   167	async function resolveSummarizeJob(
   168	  job: PgBoss.Job<SummarizeTranscriptJobData>,
   169	  infraModel: InfraModelConfig,
   170	): Promise<ResolveSummarizeJobResult> {
   171	  const { db } = await import('@valuerank/db');
   172	  const { transcriptId, summaryModelId } = job.data;
   173	  const modelId = summaryModelId ?? `${infraModel.providerName}:${infraModel.modelId}`;
   174	  const providerName = getProviderNameFromModelId(modelId, infraModel.providerName);
   175	
   176	  log.info(
   177	    { jobId: job.id, runId: job.data.runId, transcriptId, modelId },
   178	    'Processing summarize_transcript job'
   179	  );
   180	
   181	  const transcript = await db.transcript.findUnique({
   182	    where: { id: transcriptId },
   183	  });
   184	
   185	  if (!transcript) {
   186	    log.error({ jobId: job.id, transcriptId }, 'Transcript not found');
   187	    return { kind: 'missing' };
   188	  }
   189	
   190	  const wasAlreadySummarized = transcript.summarizedAt !== null;
   191	  const responseSha256 = computeTranscriptResponseSha256(transcript.content);
   192	  const transcriptDecisionMetadata = isPlainJsonObject(transcript.decisionMetadata)
   193	    ? transcript.decisionMetadata
   194	    : null;
   195	  const hasSummaryCacheField = transcriptDecisionMetadata !== null && 'summaryCache' in transcriptDecisionMetadata;
   196	  const summaryCache = hasSummaryCacheField && isSummaryCache(transcriptDecisionMetadata.summaryCache)
   197	    ? transcriptDecisionMetadata.summaryCache
   198	    : null;
   199	  const parserVersion = config.SUMMARIZE_PARSER_VERSION;
   200	  const forceSummarize = job.data.forceSummarize === true;
   201	
   202	  if (!forceSummarize && summaryCache && isCacheRecordMatch(summaryCache, responseSha256, parserVersion, modelId)) {
   203	    log.info({ jobId: job.id, transcriptId, modelId }, 'Transcript summary cache hit');
   204	
   205	    if (!wasAlreadySummarized) {
   206	      await persistCachedSummary(job, transcript, summaryCache, responseSha256, parserVersion, modelId);
   207	    }
   208	
   209	    return { kind: 'cache-hit' };
   210	  }
   211	
   212	  if (!forceSummarize && !hasSummaryCacheField && wasAlreadySummarized) {
   213	    log.info({ jobId: job.id, transcriptId }, 'Transcript already summarized, skipping');
   214	    return { kind: 'skipped' };
   215	  }
   216	
   217	  if (!forceSummarize && hasSummaryCacheField) {
   218	    log.info({ jobId: job.id, transcriptId, modelId }, 'Transcript summary cache miss, re-summarizing');
   219	  }
   220	
   221	  return {
   222	    kind: 'pending',
   223	    job: {
   224	      job,
   225	      transcript,
   226	      transcriptId,
   227	      modelId,
   228	      providerName,
   229	      responseSha256,
   230	      parserVersion,
   231	    },
   232	  };
   233	}

   313	      'Python spawn failed'
   314	    );
   315	    return handleBatchFailure(error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error)));
   316	  }
   317	
   318	  if (result === null) {
   319	    return handleBatchFailure(new Error('Python worker failed before returning a result'));
   320	  }
   321	
   322	  if (!result.success) {
   323	    log.error({ batchId, groupIndex, modelId, providerName, error: result.error, stderr: result.stderr }, 'Python spawn failed');
   324	    return handleBatchFailure(new Error(`Python worker failed: ${result.error}`));
   325	  }
   326	
   327	  const output = result.data;
   328	  let summaries: SummarizeWorkerBatchItemOutput[] | null = null;
   329	
   330	  if ('summaries' in output && Array.isArray(output.summaries)) {
   331	    summaries = output.summaries;
   332	  } else if (pendingJobs.length === 1 && 'summary' in output && output.success) {
   333	    summaries = [

    58	const EXAMPLE_LIMIT = 3;
    59	
    60	function takeLimited<T>(items: T[], item: T, limit: number): void {
    61	  if (items.length < limit) {
    62	    items.push(item);
    63	  }
    64	}
    65	
    66	function classifyBucket(result: TranscriptDecisionModelResult): DecisionModelShadowValidationBucket {
    67	  const parseClass = result.raw.parseClass;
    68	  if (parseClass === 'ambiguous') {
    69	    return 'ambiguous';
    70	  }
    71	  if (parseClass === 'unparseable') {
    72	    return 'unparseable';
    73	  }
    74	  if (parseClass === 'exact' || parseClass === 'fallback_resolved') {
    75	    if (result.canonical.source === 'deterministic' || result.canonical.source === 'manual') {
    76	      return parseClass;
    77	    }
    78	    return 'missing_metadata';
    79	  }
    80	  return 'missing_metadata';
    81	}

    84	  _transcript: DecisionModelShadowValidationTranscriptInput,

    86	  // Legacy V1 score removed — comparison is no longer applicable.
    87	  return { legacyScore: null, v2Score: null, matches: null };

   100	export function buildDecisionModelShadowValidationReport(
   101	  transcripts: DecisionModelShadowValidationTranscriptInput[],
   102	  now: Date = new Date(),
   103	): DecisionModelShadowValidationReport {
   104	  const bucketExemplars = emptyBuckets();
   105	  const comparisonMismatchExemplars: DecisionModelShadowValidationTranscript[] = [];
   106	  const transcriptResults: DecisionModelShadowValidationTranscript[] = [];
   107	
   108	  let exactCount = 0;
   109	  let fallbackResolvedCount = 0;
   110	  let ambiguousCount = 0;
   111	  let unparseableCount = 0;
   112	  let missingMetadataCount = 0;
   113	  let comparisonEligibleCount = 0;
   114	  let comparisonMismatchCount = 0;
   115	
   116	  for (const transcript of transcripts) {
   117	    const result = resolveTranscriptDecisionModel(transcript);
   118	    const bucket = classifyBucket(result);
   119	    const comparison = compareScores(transcript);
   120	    const record: DecisionModelShadowValidationTranscript = {
   121	      transcriptId: transcript.transcriptId,
   122	      runId: transcript.runId,
   123	      modelId: transcript.modelId,
   124	      scenarioId: transcript.scenarioId,
   125	      bucket,
   126	      parseClass: result.raw.parseClass,
   127	      canonicalSource: result.canonical.source,
   128	      canonical: result.canonical,
   129	      comparison,
   130	    };
   131	
   132	    transcriptResults.push(record);
   133	    takeLimited(bucketExemplars[bucket], record, EXAMPLE_LIMIT);
   134	
   135	    if (bucket === 'exact') {
   136	      exactCount += 1;
   137	    } else if (bucket === 'fallback_resolved') {
   138	      fallbackResolvedCount += 1;
   139	    } else if (bucket === 'ambiguous') {
   140	      ambiguousCount += 1;
   141	    } else if (bucket === 'unparseable') {
   142	      unparseableCount += 1;
   143	    } else {
   144	      missingMetadataCount += 1;
   145	    }
   146	
   147	    if (comparison.matches !== null) {
   148	      comparisonEligibleCount += 1;
   149	    }
   150	    if (comparison.matches === false) {
   151	      comparisonMismatchCount += 1;
   152	      takeLimited(comparisonMismatchExemplars, record, EXAMPLE_LIMIT);
   153	    }
   154	  }
   155	
   156	  return {
   157	    generatedAt: now.toISOString(),
   158	    transcriptCount: transcriptResults.length,
   159	    exactCount,
   160	    fallbackResolvedCount,
   161	    ambiguousCount,
   162	    unparseableCount,
   163	    missingMetadataCount,
   164	    comparisonEligibleCount,
   165	    comparisonMismatchCount,
   166	    bucketExemplars,
   167	    comparisonMismatchExemplars,
   168	    transcripts: transcriptResults,
   169	  };
   170	}

 succeeded in 0ms:
   240	
   241	    First looks for structured "Rating: X" format (most reliable).
   242	    Falls back to finding first standalone positive integer (less reliable).
   243	
   244	    Returns None if no rating found.
   245	    """
   246	    if not text:
   247	        return None
   248	
   249	    # Strip lightweight markdown markers that often surround numeric answers.
   250	    sanitized_markdown_text = text.replace("**", "").replace("__", "").replace("`", "")
   251	
   252	    # First, try structured "Rating: X" format (most reliable)
   253	    structured_match = STRUCTURED_RATING_PATTERN.search(sanitized_markdown_text)
   254	    if structured_match:
   255	        suffix = sanitized_markdown_text[structured_match.end():structured_match.end() + 24]
   256	        if AMBIGUOUS_SUFFIX_PATTERN.search(suffix):
   257	            return None
   258	        return structured_match.group(1)
   259	
   260	    # Next, look for common explicit decision formats.
   261	    for pattern in STRUCTURED_DECISION_PATTERNS:
   262	        matches = []
   263	        for match in pattern.finditer(sanitized_markdown_text):
   264	            # If immediate continuation suggests multiple candidate codes
   265	            # (e.g., "I choose 3 and 4"), treat as ambiguous.
   266	            suffix = sanitized_markdown_text[match.end():match.end() + 24]
   267	            if AMBIGUOUS_SUFFIX_PATTERN.search(suffix):
   268	                return None
   269	            matches.append(match.group(1))
   270	        if not matches:
   271	            continue
   272	        unique_values = list(dict.fromkeys(matches))
   273	        if len(unique_values) == 1:
   274	            return unique_values[0]
   275	        # If an explicit format provides conflicting values, treat as ambiguous.
   276	        return None
   277	
   278	    # Remove numeric ranges (e.g., "1-6", "1 to 6") before fallback scanning.
   279	    sanitized_text = RANGE_PATTERN.sub(" ", sanitized_markdown_text)
   280	    # Strip word-count parentheticals like "(5 words)" before fallback scanning.
   281	    # Some models append these as metadata; a coincidentally valid code would cause
   282	    # a false positive that the out-of-range guard cannot catch.
   283	    sanitized_text = WORD_COUNT_SUFFIX_PATTERN.sub(" ", sanitized_text)
   284	
   285	    fallback_matches = [m.group(1) for m in FALLBACK_RATING_PATTERN.finditer(sanitized_text)]
   286	    if not fallback_matches:
   287	        if REFUSAL_PATTERN.search(text):
   288	            return "refusal"
   289	        return None
   290	
   291	    # If the model enumerates multiple options (e.g., "1..6"), it did not choose one.
   292	    unique_values = list(dict.fromkeys(fallback_matches))
   293	    if len(unique_values) > 1:
   294	        return None
   295	
   296	    # If response is clearly directed at the user and lacks self-rating language,
   297	    # treat as no valid decision choice.
   298	    lower_text = text.lower()
   299	    has_user_directed = USER_DIRECTED_PATTERN.search(lower_text) is not None
   300	    has_self_rating = SELF_RATING_PATTERN.search(lower_text) is not None
   301	    if has_user_directed and not has_self_rating:
   302	        return None
   303	
   304	    return unique_values[0]
   305	
   306	
   307	def extract_explicit_leading_decision_code(text: str) -> Optional[str]:
   308	    """
   309	    Extract a decision from a leading candidate only when the candidate contains
   310	    an explicit decision signal.
   311	
   312	    This intentionally avoids the broad fallback number scan used for whole-response
   313	    parsing, because opening lines often contain contextual numbers that are not
   314	    the final decision.
   315	    """
   316	    if not text:
   317	        return None
   318	
   319	    sanitized_markdown_text = text.replace("**", "").replace("__", "").replace("`", "")
   320	
   321	    structured_match = STRUCTURED_RATING_PATTERN.search(sanitized_markdown_text)
   322	    if structured_match:
   323	        suffix = sanitized_markdown_text[structured_match.end():structured_match.end() + 24]
   324	        if AMBIGUOUS_SUFFIX_PATTERN.search(suffix):
   325	            return None
   326	        return structured_match.group(1)
   327	
   328	    for pattern in STRUCTURED_DECISION_PATTERNS:
   329	        matches = []
   330	        for match in pattern.finditer(sanitized_markdown_text):
   331	            suffix = sanitized_markdown_text[match.end():match.end() + 24]
   332	            if AMBIGUOUS_SUFFIX_PATTERN.search(suffix):
   333	                return None
   334	            matches.append(match.group(1))
   335	        if not matches:
   336	            continue
   337	        unique_values = list(dict.fromkeys(matches))
   338	        if len(unique_values) == 1:
   339	            return unique_values[0]
   340	        return None
   341	
   342	    bare_number_match = LEADING_BARE_NUMBER_PATTERN.match(sanitized_markdown_text)
   343	    if bare_number_match:
   344	        return bare_number_match.group(1)
   345	
   346	    if REFUSAL_PATTERN.search(text):
   347	        return "refusal"
   348	
   349	    return None
   350	
   351	
   352	def extract_decision_code(transcript_content: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
   353	    """
   354	    Extract numeric decision code (positive integer) from transcript.
   355	
   356	    Looks for "Rating: X" format first (structured response from probe).
   357	    Falls back to finding first positive integer in the response.
   358	
   359	    Returns "other" if no clear rating/refusal found.
   360	    """
   361	    turns = transcript_content.get("turns", [])
   362	
   363	    # Combine all target responses
   364	    full_text = ""
   365	    for turn in turns:
   366	        response = turn.get("targetResponse", "")
   367	        if response:
   368	            full_text += response + "\n"
   369	
   370	    result = extract_decision_code_from_text(full_text)
   371	    return result if result else "other"

    47	function isNumericDecisionValue(decisionValue: string | number | null | undefined): boolean {
    48	  return decisionValue === '1'
    49	    || decisionValue === '2'
    50	    || decisionValue === '3'
    51	    || decisionValue === '4'
    52	    || decisionValue === '5'

    60	function hasMeaningfulMetadata(transcript: Transcript): boolean {
    61	  const metadata = getDecisionMetadata(transcript.decisionMetadata);
    62	  if (!metadata) {
    63	    return false;
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  return Boolean(
    67	    metadata.parseClass ||
    68	      metadata.parsePath ||
    69	      metadata.parserVersion ||
    70	      metadata.matchedLabel ||
    71	      metadata.responseExcerpt ||
    72	      metadata.responseSha256 ||
    73	      metadata.manualOverride ||
    74	      (metadata.scaleLabels && metadata.scaleLabels.length > 0)
    75	  );
    76	}

    78	export function summarizeDecisionCoverage(transcripts: Transcript[]): DecisionCoverageSummary {
    79	  const summary: DecisionCoverageSummary = {
    80	    totalTranscripts: 0,
    81	    scoredTranscripts: 0,
    82	    unresolvedTranscripts: 0,
    83	    parserScoredTranscripts: 0,
    84	    manuallyAdjudicatedTranscripts: 0,
    85	    exactMatchTranscripts: 0,
    86	    fallbackResolvedTranscripts: 0,
    87	    ambiguousTranscripts: 0,
    88	    legacyNumericTranscripts: 0,
    89	    hasMethodologySignals: false,
    90	    perModel: {},
    91	  };
    92	
    93	  for (const transcript of transcripts) {
    94	    const modelId = transcript.modelId;
    95	    const perModel = summary.perModel[modelId] ?? createEmptyModelCoverage(modelId);
    96	    summary.perModel[modelId] = perModel;
    97	
    98	    const metadata = getDecisionMetadata(transcript.decisionMetadata);
    99	    const parseClass = metadata?.parseClass;
   100	    const hasManualOverride = Boolean(metadata?.manualOverride);
   101	    const isScored = isNumericDecisionValue(getTranscriptDecisionSortValue(transcript, 'legacy'));
   102	
   103	    summary.totalTranscripts += 1;
   104	    perModel.totalTranscripts += 1;
   105	
   106	    if (hasMeaningfulMetadata(transcript)) {
   107	      summary.hasMethodologySignals = true;
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    if (parseClass === 'ambiguous') {
   111	      summary.ambiguousTranscripts += 1;
   112	      perModel.ambiguousTranscripts += 1;
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    if (isScored) {
   116	      summary.scoredTranscripts += 1;
   117	      perModel.scoredTranscripts += 1;
   118	
   119	      if (hasManualOverride) {
   120	        summary.manuallyAdjudicatedTranscripts += 1;
   121	        perModel.manuallyAdjudicatedTranscripts += 1;
   122	        continue;
   123	      }
   124	
   125	      if (parseClass === 'exact') {
   126	        summary.parserScoredTranscripts += 1;
   127	        summary.exactMatchTranscripts += 1;
   128	        perModel.parserScoredTranscripts += 1;
   129	        perModel.exactMatchTranscripts += 1;
   130	        continue;
   131	      }
   132	
   133	      if (parseClass === 'fallback_resolved') {
   134	        summary.parserScoredTranscripts += 1;
   135	        summary.fallbackResolvedTranscripts += 1;
   136	        perModel.parserScoredTranscripts += 1;
   137	        perModel.fallbackResolvedTranscripts += 1;
   138	        continue;
   139	      }
   140	
   141	      summary.legacyNumericTranscripts += 1;
   142	      perModel.legacyNumericTranscripts += 1;
   143	      continue;
   144	    }
   145	
   146	    summary.unresolvedTranscripts += 1;
   147	    perModel.unresolvedTranscripts += 1;
   148	  }
   149	
   150	  return summary;
   151	}
   152	
   153	function normalizeModelId(modelId: string): string {
   154	  const parts = modelId.split(':');
   155	  return parts[parts.length - 1] ?? modelId;
   156	}
   157	
   158	export function getCoverageForModel(
   159	  coverage: DecisionCoverageSummary | null | undefined,
   160	  modelId: string,
   161	): ModelDecisionCoverage | null {
   162	  if (!coverage) {
   163	    return null;
   164	  }
   165	
   166	  if (coverage.perModel[modelId]) {
   167	    return coverage.perModel[modelId] ?? null;
   168	  }
   169	
   170	  const normalizedModelId = normalizeModelId(modelId);
   171	  const matchedEntry = Object.values(coverage.perModel).find(
   172	    (entry) => normalizeModelId(entry.modelId) === normalizedModelId,
   173	  );
   174	
   175	  return matchedEntry ?? null;
   176	}
   177	
   178	export function shouldShowDecisionCoverage(coverage: DecisionCoverageSummary | null | undefined): boolean {
   179	  if (!coverage) {
   180	    return false;
   181	  }
   182	
   183	  return coverage.hasMethodologySignals || coverage.unresolvedTranscripts > 0 || coverage.manuallyAdjudicatedTranscripts > 0;
   184	}

   102	      ) {
   103	        acc.unresolved += 1;
   104	      }
   105	      return acc;
   106	    },
   107	    { exact: 0, fallback: 0, ambiguous: 0, manual: 0, unresolved: 0 }
   108	  );
   109	
   110	  const listDisplayMode = 'audit' as const;
   111	  const viewerDisplayMode = 'audit' as const;
   112	  const decisionColumnLabel = 'Decision summary';
   113	  const decisionColumnTooltip = 'Shows the canonical decision headline and summary from the backend transcript data.';
   114	
   115	  const backButton = (
   116	    <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
   117	      <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => navigate(-1)}>
   118	        <ArrowLeft className="w-4 h-4 mr-1" />
   119	        Back
   120	      </Button>
   121	    </div>
   122	  );
   123	
   124	  if (loading && !run) {
   125	    return (
   126	      <div className="space-y-6">
   127	        {backButton}
   128	        <Loading size="lg" text="Loading transcripts..." />
   129	      </div>
   130	    );

codex
I’ve got enough context to write the review. The main risks are all around undercounting: the spec narrows “unresolvable” more than the existing code does, and it uses one field name the worker does not emit.
codex
## Findings
- High: [CODE-CONFIRMED] The spec’s “unresolvable” definition is too narrow. `persistSummarizeFailure` still sets `summarizedAt` when a summarize job fails, but the spec only counts `decision_code`, cached `decisionState`, or `parseClass`. That means failed summaries will be invisible to the new warning. The repo also already treats `parseClass === 'unparseable'` and `canonical.source === 'error'` as unresolved in the existing coverage UI, so this spec would undercount both failed jobs and legacy bad rows. [summarize-persistence.ts](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/practical-noyce-1db12d/cloud/apps/api/src/queue/handlers/summarize-persistence.ts#L250) [analysisCoverage.ts](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/practical-noyce-1db12d/cloud/apps/web/src/utils/analysisCoverage.ts#L78) [AnalysisTranscripts.tsx](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/practical-noyce-1db12d/cloud/apps/web/src/pages/AnalysisTranscripts.tsx#L84)

- Medium: [CODE-CONFIRMED] The spec uses `decisionCodeSource`, but the worker returns `decisionSource`, and only the persistence layer renames that into stored `decisionCodeSource`. The spec needs to pin which layer it is talking about, or implementation/tests will assert the wrong field name. [summarize.py](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/practical-noyce-1db12d/cloud/workers/summarize.py#L159) [summarize-persistence.ts](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/practical-noyce-1db12d/cloud/apps/api/src/queue/handlers/summarize-persistence.ts#L40)

- Medium: [CODE-CONFIRMED] The per-model breakdown is underspecified for model aliasing and provider prefixes. The summarize handler persists prefixed IDs like `provider:model`, while the existing coverage helper normalizes model IDs when matching counts. A naïve exact-string breakdown in the new warning can split one logical model across multiple buckets or disagree with other run pages. [summarize-transcript.ts](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/practical-noyce-1db12d/cloud/apps/api/src/queue/handlers/summarize-transcript.ts#L172) [analysisCoverage.ts](/Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/practical-noyce-1db12d/cloud/apps/web/src/utils/analysisCoverage.ts#L153)

## Residual Risks
- I could not verify the exact run-detail API/MCP response shape from the provided code, so there is still integration risk in how the new count is surfaced.
- If the intent is to define a narrower warning than the existing “unresolved transcript” UI, that policy needs to be stated explicitly; otherwise different pages will keep counting different things.
